# Liquid objects: metaobject_definition

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metaobject_definition#main-content)

A `metaobject_definition` defines the structure of a metaobject type for the store, which consists of a merchant-defined set of [field definitions](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/metafields/metafield-definitions)
.

One or more corresponding [`metaobject`](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects#metaobject)
 objects contain values for the fields specified in the metaobject definition.

* * *

Note

When looping through metaobjects by accessing them using individual handles (e.g., `metaobjects.TYPE[handle]`), you're limited to 20 unique handles per page and can't use [pagination](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/tags/paginate)
. To iterate over more metaobjects, instead use the `values` property, which supports pagination up to 250 entries per page.

**Note:**

When looping through metaobjects by accessing them using individual handles (e.g., `metaobjects.TYPE[handle]`), you're limited to 20 unique handles per page and can't use [pagination](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/tags/paginate)
. To iterate over more metaobjects, instead use the `values` property, which supports pagination up to 250 entries per page.

**Note:** When looping through metaobjects by accessing them using individual handles (e.g., <code><span class="PreventFireFoxApplyingGapToWBR">metaobjects.T<wbr/>Y<wbr/>P<wbr/>E\[handle\]</span></code>), you&#39;re limited to 20 unique handles per page and can&#39;t use <a href="/docs/api/liquid/tags/paginate">pagination</a>. To iterate over more metaobjects, instead use the <code>values</code> property, which supports pagination up to 250 entries per page.

* * *

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metaobject_definition#metaobject_definition-values)

values**values**

array of [metaobject](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metaobject)

The [metaobjects](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects#metaobject)
 that follow the definition.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metaobject_definition#metaobject_definition-values_count)

values\_count**values\_count**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The total number of entries for the metaobject definition.

[Anchor to Loop over entries of a metaobject definition](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metaobject_definition#metaobject_definition-loop-over-entries-of-a-metaobject-definition)

### 

Loop over entries of a metaobject definition

If a metaobject definition has multiple metaobject entries, then you can loop over them using the `values` property. You can loop over a maximum of 50 entries in a metaobject definition. For example, you can display the field `author` for each metaobject using the following `forloop`:

9

1

2

3

{% for testimonial in metaobjects.testimonials.values %}

{{ testimonial.author.value }}

{% endfor %}

    {% for testimonial in metaobjects.testimonials.values %}
      {{ testimonial.author.value }}
    {% endfor %}

* * *

Note

When the [`publishable` capability](https://shopify.dev/apps/data-extensions/metaobjects/capabilities)
 is enabled, loops return only metaobjects with a status of `active`. Metaobjects with a status of `draft` are skipped.

**Note:**

When the [`publishable` capability](https://shopify.dev/apps/data-extensions/metaobjects/capabilities)
 is enabled, loops return only metaobjects with a status of `active`. Metaobjects with a status of `draft` are skipped.

**Note:** When the <a href="/apps/data-extensions/metaobjects/capabilities"><code>publishable</code> capability</a> is enabled, loops return only metaobjects with a status of <code>active</code>. Metaobjects with a status of <code>draft</code> are skipped.

* * *

Was this section helpful?

YesNo

---

# Liquid objects: part

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/part#main-content)

A part in the navigation for pagination.

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/part#part-is_link)

is\_link**is\_link**

[boolean](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#boolean)

Returns `true` if the part is a link. Returns `false` if not.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/part#part-title)

title**title**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The page number associated with the part.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/part#part-url)

url**url**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The URL of the part.

It consists of the current page URL path with the pagination parameter for the current part appended.

9

1

2

3

4

5

{

"is\_link": true,

"title": "2",

"url": "/collections/all?page=2"

}

##### Example

    {
      "is_link": true,
      "title": "2",
      "url": "/collections/all?page=2"
    }

[Anchor to Create pagination navigation with \`part\`](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/part#part-create-pagination-navigation-with-part)

### 

Create pagination navigation with `part`

You can create a pagination navigation by iterating over each `part` of a [`paginate` object](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/paginate)
.

9

1

2

3

4

5

6

7

8

9

{% paginate collection.products by 5 \-%}

{% for part in paginate.parts \-%}

{% if part.is\_link \-%}

{{ part.title | link\_to: part.url}}

{%- else \-%}

<span\>{{ part.title }}</span\>

{% endif %}

{%- endfor %}

{%- endpaginate %}

##### Code

    {% paginate collection.products by 5 -%}
      {% for part in paginate.parts -%}
        {% if part.is_link -%}
          {{ part.title | link_to: part.url}}
        {%- else -%}
          <span>{{ part.title }}</span>
        {% endif %}
      {%- endfor %}
    {%- endpaginate %}

##### Data

    {
      "collection": {
        "products_count": 19
      }
    }

Output
------

9

1

2

3

4

5

6

7

<span\>1</span\>

<a href\="/services/liquid\_rendering/resource?page=2" title\=""\>2</a\>

  

<a href\="/services/liquid\_rendering/resource?page=3" title\=""\>3</a\>

  

<a href\="/services/liquid\_rendering/resource?page=4" title\=""\>4</a\>

##### Output

    <span>1</span>
        
    <a href="/services/liquid_rendering/resource?page=2" title="">2</a>
    
    <a href="/services/liquid_rendering/resource?page=3" title="">3</a>
    
    <a href="/services/liquid_rendering/resource?page=4" title="">4</a>

# Liquid objects: country

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#main-content)

A country supported by the store's localization options.

To learn how to use the `country` object to offer localization options in your theme, refer to [Support multiple currencies and languages](https://shopify.dev/themes/internationalization/multiple-currencies-languages)
.

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-available_languages)

available\_languages**available\_languages**

array of [shop\_locale](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale)

The languages that have been added to the market that this country belongs to.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-continent)

continent**continent**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The continent that the country is in.

Possible values are `Africa`, `Asia`, `Central America`, `Europe`, `North America`, `Oceania`, and `South America`.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-currency)

currency**currency**

[currency](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/currency)

The currency used in the country.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-iso_code)

iso\_code**iso\_code**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The ISO code of the country in [ISO 3166-1 (alpha 2) format](https://www.iso.org/glossary-for-iso-3166.html)
.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-market)

market**market**

[market](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/market)

The market that includes this country.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-name)

name**name**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The name of the country.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-popular?)

popular?**popular?**

[boolean](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#boolean)

Returns `true` if the country is popular for this shop. Otherwise, returns `false`. This can be useful for sorting countries in a country selector.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/country#country-unit_system)

unit\_system**unit\_system**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)
 from a set of values

The unit system of the country.

| Possible values |
| --- |
| imperial |
| metric |

### 

Rendering a flag image

When the country object is passed to the [`image_url`](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/filters#image_url)
 filter, a [CDN URL](https://shopify.dev/themes/best-practices/performance/platform#shopify-cdn)
 for that country’s flag is returned. All country’s flags are SVGs, normalized to an aspect ratio of 4:3.

9

1

{{ localization.country | image\_url: width: 32 | image\_tag }}

##### Code

    {{ localization.country | image_url: width: 32 | image_tag }}

##### Data

    {
      "localization": {
        "country": "Canada"
      }
    }

------

9

1

<img src\="//cdn.shopify.com/static/images/flags/ca.svg?width=32" alt\="Canada" srcset\="//cdn.shopify.com/static/images/flags/ca.svg?width=32 32w" width\="32" height\="24"\>

##### Output

    <img src="//cdn.shopify.com/static/images/flags/ca.svg?width=32" alt="Canada" srcset="//cdn.shopify.com/static/images/flags/ca.svg?width=32 32w" width="32" height="24">

# Liquid objects: recommendations

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/recommendations#main-content)

Product recommendations for a specific product based on sales data, product descriptions, and collection relationships.

Product recommendations become more accurate over time as new orders and product data become available. To learn more about how product recommendations are generated, refer to [Product recommendations](https://shopify.dev/themes/product-merchandising/recommendations)
.

* * *

Note

The `recommendations` object returns products only when rendered in a section using the [Product Recommendations API](https://shopify.dev/api/ajax/reference/product-recommendations)
 and the [Section Rendering API](https://shopify.dev/api/section-rendering)
. To learn about how to include product recommendations in your theme, refer to [Show product recommendations](https://shopify.dev/themes/product-merchandising/recommendations/show-product-recommendations)
.

**Note:**

The `recommendations` object returns products only when rendered in a section using the [Product Recommendations API](https://shopify.dev/api/ajax/reference/product-recommendations)
 and the [Section Rendering API](https://shopify.dev/api/section-rendering)
. To learn about how to include product recommendations in your theme, refer to [Show product recommendations](https://shopify.dev/themes/product-merchandising/recommendations/show-product-recommendations)
.

**Note:** The <code>recommendations</code> object returns products only when rendered in a section using the <a href="/api/ajax/reference/product-recommendations">Product Recommendations API</a> and the <a href="/api/section-rendering">Section Rendering API</a>. To learn about how to include product recommendations in your theme, refer to <a href="/themes/product-merchandising/recommendations/show-product-recommendations">Show product recommendations</a>.

* * *

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/recommendations#recommendations-intent)

intent**intent**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The recommendation intent.

If `performed?` is `false`, then `nil` is returned.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/recommendations#recommendations-performed?)

performed?**performed?**

[boolean](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#boolean)

Returns `true` when being referenced inside a section that's been rendered using the Product Recommendations API and the Section Rendering API. Returns `false` if not.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/recommendations#recommendations-products)

products**products**

array of [product](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/product)

The recommended products.

If `performed?` is `false`, then an [EmptyDrop](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#emptydrop)
 is returned.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/recommendations#recommendations-products_count)

products\_count**products\_count**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The number of recommended products.

If `performed?` is `false`, then 0 is returned.

9

1

2

3

4

5

{

"products": \[\],

"products\_count": 4,

"performed?": true

}

##### Example

    {
      "products": [],
      "products_count": 4,
      "performed?": true
    }

# Liquid objects: quantity_price_break

price**price**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The value is the price in the customer's local (presentment) currency.

# Liquid objects: quantity_rule

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/quantity_rule#main-content)

A variant order quantity rule.

If no rule exists, then a default value is returned.

This rule can be set as part of a [B2B catalog](https://help.shopify.com/manual/b2b/catalogs/quantity-pricing)
.

* * *

Note

The default quantity rule is `min=1,max=null,increment=1`.

**Note:**

The default quantity rule is `min=1,max=null,increment=1`.

**Note:** The default quantity rule is <code>min=1,max=null,increment=1</code>.

* * *

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/quantity_rule#quantity_rule-increment)

increment**increment**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The number the order quantity can be incremented by. The default value is `1`.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/quantity_rule#quantity_rule-max)

max**max**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The maximum order quantity.

If there is no maximum quantity, then `nil` is returned.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/quantity_rule#quantity_rule-min)

min**min**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The minimum order quantity. The default value is `1`.

# Liquid objects: shop_locale

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#main-content)

A language in a store.

To learn how to offer localization options in your theme, refer to [Support multiple currencies and languages](https://shopify.dev/themes/internationalization/multiple-currencies-languages)
.

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#shop_locale-endonym_name)

endonym\_name**endonym\_name**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The name of the locale in the locale itself.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#shop_locale-iso_code)

iso\_code**iso\_code**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The ISO code of the locale in [IETF language tag format](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IETF_language_tag)
.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#shop_locale-name)

name**name**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The name of the locale in the store's primary locale.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#shop_locale-primary)

primary**primary**

[boolean](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#boolean)

Returns `true` if the locale is the store's primary locale. Returns `false` if not.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/shop_locale#shop_locale-root_url)

root\_url**root\_url**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The relative root URL of the locale.

9

1

2

3

4

5

6

7

{

"endonym\_name": "English",

"iso\_code": "en",

"name": "English",

"primary": true,

"root\_url": "/"

}

##### Example

    {
      "endonym_name": "English",
      "iso_code": "en",
      "name": "English",
      "primary": true,
      "root_url": "/"
    }

# Liquid objects: pages

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/pages#main-content)

All of the [pages](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page)
 on a store.

### Directly accessible in

*   Global

You can access a specific page through the `pages` object using the page's [handle](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#handles)
.

9

1

2

{{ pages.contact.title }}

{{ pages\['about-us'\].title }}

##### Code

    {{ pages.contact.title }}
    {{ pages['about-us'].title }}

Output
------

9

1

2

Contact

About us

##### Output

    Contact
    About us

[Anchor to Paginate the \`pages\` object](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/pages#pages-paginate-the-pages-object)

### 

Paginate the `pages` object

You can [paginate](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/tags/paginate)
 the `pages` object, allowing you to iterate over up to 50 pages at a time.

9

1

2

3

4

5

6

7

{% paginate pages by 2 \-%}

{% for page in pages \-%}

{{ page.title | link\_to: page.url }}

{%- endfor %}

  

{{- paginate | default\_pagination }}

{%- endpaginate %}

##### Code

    {% paginate pages by 2 -%}
      {% for page in pages -%}
        {{ page.title | link_to: page.url }}
      {%- endfor %}
    
      {{- paginate | default_pagination }}
    {%- endpaginate %}

Output
------

9

1

2

3

4

<a href\="/pages/about-us" title\=""\>About us</a\>

<a href\="/pages/contact" title\=""\>Contact</a\>

  

<span class\="page current"\>1</span\> <span class\="page"\><a href\="/services/liquid\_rendering/resource?page=2" title\=""\>2</a\></span\> <span class\="next"\><a href\="/services/liquid\_rendering/resource?page=2" title\=""\>Next &raquo;</a\></span\>

##### Output

    <a href="/pages/about-us" title="">About us</a>
    <a href="/pages/contact" title="">Contact</a>
    
    <span class="page current">1</span> <span class="page"><a href="/services/liquid_rendering/resource?page=2" title="">2</a></span> <span class="next"><a href="/services/liquid_rendering/resource?page=2" title="">Next &raquo;</a></span>

Was this section helpful?

YesNo

# Liquid objects: page

[Skip to main content](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#main-content)

A [page](https://help.shopify.com/manual/online-store/themes/theme-structure/pages)
 on a store.

Properties
----------

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-author)

author**author**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The author of the page.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-content)

content**content**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The content of the page.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-handle)

handle**handle**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The [handle](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#handles)
 of the page.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-id)

id**id**

[number](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#number)

The ID of the page.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-metafields)

metafields**metafields**

The [metafields](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/metafield)
 applied to the page.

Tip

To learn about how to create metafields, refer to [Create and manage metafields](https://shopify.dev/apps/metafields/manage)
 or visit the [Shopify Help Center](https://help.shopify.com/manual/metafields)
.

**Tip:**

To learn about how to create metafields, refer to [Create and manage metafields](https://shopify.dev/apps/metafields/manage)
 or visit the [Shopify Help Center](https://help.shopify.com/manual/metafields)
.

**Tip:** To learn about how to create metafields, refer to <a href="/apps/metafields/manage">Create and manage metafields</a> or visit the <a href="https://help.shopify.com/manual/metafields">Shopify Help Center</a>.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-published_at)

published\_at**published\_at**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

A timestamp for when the page was published.

Tip

Use the [`date` filter](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/filters/date)
 to format the timestamp.

**Tip:**

Use the [`date` filter](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/filters/date)
 to format the timestamp.

**Tip:** Use the <a href="/docs/api/liquid/filters/date"><code>date</code> filter</a> to format the timestamp.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-template_suffix)

template\_suffix**template\_suffix**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The name of the [custom template](https://shopify.dev/themes/architecture/templates#alternate-templates)
 assigned to the page.

The name doesn't include the `page.` prefix, or the file extension (`.json` or `.liquid`).

If a custom template isn't assigned to the page, then `nil` is returned.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-title)

title**title**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The title of the page.

[Anchor to](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/objects/page#page-url)

url**url**

[string](https://shopify.dev/docs/api/liquid/basics#string)

The relative URL of the page.

99

3

5

8

9

10

"author": null,

"content": "<p>Polina's Potent Potions was started by Polina in 1654.</p>\\n<p>We use all-natural locally sourced ingredients for our potions.</p>",

"handle": "about-us",

"id": 83536642113,

"metafields": {},

"published\_at": "2022-05-04 17:47:03 -0400",

"template\_suffix": "",

"title": "About us",

"url": {}

}

##### Example

    {
      "author": null,
      "content": "<p>Polina's Potent Potions was started by Polina in 1654.</p>\n<p>We use all-natural locally sourced ingredients for our potions.</p>",
      "handle": "about-us",
      "id": 83536642113,
      "metafields": {},
      "published_at": "2022-05-04 17:47:03 -0400",
      "template_suffix": "",
      "title": "About us",
      "url": {}
    }
